Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Public Education System -- State Administration
=================================================================================

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 1 - Title Provisions
**************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-101(1): This title is known as "Public Education System -- State Administration."
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-101(2): This chapter is known as "Title Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102 Public education code definitions.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Unless otherwise indicated, as used in this title,Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(1): 53G-5-303 "Charter agreement" means an agreement made in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(2): "Charter school governing board" means the board that governs a charter school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(3): "District school" means a public school under the control of a local school board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(4): "Individualized education program" or "IEP" means a written statement for a student with a disability that is developed, reviewed, and revised in accordance with the Individuals with Disabilities Education Act, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1400 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(5): "LEA governing board" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(5)(a): for a school district, the local school board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(5)(b): for a charter school, the charter school governing board; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(5)(c): for the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind, the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(6): "Local education agency" or "LEA" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(6)(a): a school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(6)(b): a charter school; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(6)(c): the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(7): Title 20A, Chapter 14, Part 2, Election of Members of Local Boards of Education "Local school board" means a board elected under
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(8): 53F-2-102 "Minimum School Program" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(9): "Parent" means a parent or legal guardian.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(10): Title 53F, Public Education System -- Funding; Title 53G, Public Education System -- Local Administration "Public education code" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(10)(a): this title;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(10)(b): Title 53F, Public Education System -- Funding
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(10)(c): Title 53G, Public Education System -- Local Administration
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(11): "Section 504 accommodation plan" means a plan developed in accordance with Section 504 of the Rehabilitation Act of 1973, 29 U.S.C. Sec. 701 et seq., for a student with a disability, to meet the student's educational needs and ensure equitable access to a free appropriate public education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(12): Title 58, Chapter 31b, Nurse Practice Act; 58-31e-102 "School nurse" means a registered nurse:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(12)(a): Title 58, Chapter 31b, Nurse Practice Act; 58-31e-102 who holds:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(12)(a)(i): Title 58, Chapter 31b, Nurse Practice Act a license under
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(12)(a)(ii): 58-31e-102 a multistate license as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(12)(b): whose primary role is the care of a defined group of students enrolled in the public school system.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(13): "State board" means the State Board of Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-102(14): 53E-3-301 "State superintendent" means the state superintendent of public instruction appointed under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203 State Superintendent's Annual Report.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1): (4)(b); (4)(a); 53G-11-511; 53E-4-301 The state board shall prepare and submit to the governor, the Education Interim Committee, and the Public Education Appropriations Subcommittee, by January 15 of each year, an annual written report known as the State Superintendent's Annual Report that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(a): the operations, activities, programs, and services of the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(b): (4)(b); (4)(a) subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c): 53G-11-511; 53E-4-301 data on the general condition of the schools with recommendations considered desirable for specific programs, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(i): a complete statement of fund balances;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(ii): a complete statement of revenues by fund and source;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(iii): a complete statement of adjusted expenditures by fund, the status of bonded indebtedness, the cost of new school plants, and school levies;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(iv): a complete statement of state funds allocated to each school district and charter school by source, including supplemental appropriations, and a complete statement of expenditures by each school district and charter school, including supplemental appropriations, by function and object as outlined in the United States Department of Education publication "Financial Accounting for Local and State School Systems";
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v): 53G-11-511; 53E-4-301 a statement that includes data on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(A): fall enrollments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(B): average membership;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(C): high school graduates;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(D): 53G-11-511 licensed and classified employees, including data reported by school districts on educator ratings described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(E): pupil-teacher ratios;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(F): average class sizes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(G): average salaries;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(H): applicable private school data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(v)(I): 53E-4-301 data from statewide assessments described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(vi): statistical information regarding incidents of delinquent activity in the schools or at school-related activities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(1)(c)(vii): other statistical and financial information about the school system that the state superintendent considers pertinent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2): (1)(c)(v)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(a): (1)(c)(v) For the purposes of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(a)(i): the pupil-teacher ratio for a school shall be calculated by dividing the number of students enrolled in a school by the number of full-time equivalent teachers assigned to the school, including regular classroom teachers, school-based specialists, and special education teachers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(a)(ii): the pupil-teacher ratio for a school district shall be the median pupil-teacher ratio of the schools within a school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(a)(iii): the pupil-teacher ratio for charter schools aggregated shall be the median pupil-teacher ratio of charter schools in the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(a)(iv): the pupil-teacher ratio for the state's public schools aggregated shall be the median pupil-teacher ratio of public schools in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b): The report shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b)(i): include the pupil-teacher ratio for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b)(i)(A): each school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b)(i)(B): the charter schools aggregated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b)(i)(C): the state's public schools aggregated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(2)(b)(ii): identify a website where pupil-teacher ratios for each school in the state may be accessed.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3): (3)(b); (c) For each operation, activity, program, or service provided by the state board, the annual report shall include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(a): a description of the operation, activity, program, or service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(b): data and metrics:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(b)(i): selected and used by the state board to measure progress, performance, effectiveness, and scope of the operation, activity, program, or service, including summary data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(b)(ii): that are consistent and comparable for each state operation, activity, program, or service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(c): budget data, including the amount and source of funding, expenses, and allocation of full-time employees for the operation, activity, program, or service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(d): (3)(b); (c) historical data from previous years for comparison with data reported under Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(e): goals, challenges, and achievements related to the operation, activity, program, or service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(f): relevant federal and state statutory references and requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(g): contact information of officials knowledgeable and responsible for each operation, activity, program, or service; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(h): other information determined by the state board that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(h)(i): may be needed, useful, or of historical significance; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-203(3)(h)(ii): promotes accountability and transparency for each operation, activity, program, or service with the public and elected officials.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205 Reporting impact analysis.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(1): As used in this section, "proposed report" means a report that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(1)(a): an LEA is required to prepare or submit to the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(1)(b): a rule proposed by the state board requires; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(1)(c): is not required by federal law, Utah Code, or another state entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(2): The state board shall establish a policy or procedures to evaluate the impact a proposed report may have on reporting requirements for an LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(3): (2) The impact described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(3)(a): the estimated cost to an LEA associated with the proposed report;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(3)(b): the estimated time an LEA administrator will spend preparing the proposed report; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-205(3)(c): any disproportionate impact the proposed report may have on an LEA because of the LEA's size, location, or other factors.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206 State board report on intergenerational poverty mitigation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(1): 35A-9-102; 35A-9-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(1)(a): 35A-9-102 "Cycle of poverty" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(1)(b): 35A-9-102 "Intergenerational poverty" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(2): 35A-9-202 On or before October 1 of each year, the state board shall provide an annual report to the Department of Workforce Services for inclusion in the intergenerational poverty report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(3): The report shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(3)(a): describe policies, procedures, and programs that the state board has implemented or modified to help break the cycle of poverty and end welfare dependency for children in the state affected by intergenerational poverty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-1-206(3)(b): contain recommendations to the Legislature on how to address issues relating to breaking the cycle of poverty and ending welfare dependency for children in the state affected by intergenerational poverty.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 2 - Public Education System Policy
****************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Public Education System Policy."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201 Policy for Utah's public education system.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(a): The continuous cultivation of an informed and virtuous citizenry among succeeding generations is essential to the state and the nation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(b): The state's public education system is established and maintained as provided in Utah Constitution, Article X, and this public education code.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(c): Parents have the primary responsibility for the education of their children and elect representatives in the Legislature and on state and local school boards to administer the state public education system, which provides extensive support and assistance.  All children of the state are entitled to a free elementary and secondary public education as provided in Utah Constitution, Article X.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(d): Public schools fulfill a vital purpose in the education and preparation of informed and responsible citizens who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(d)(i): fully understand and lawfully exercise their individual rights and liberties;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(d)(ii): become self-reliant and able to provide for themselves and their families; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(1)(d)(iii): contribute to the public good and the health, welfare, and security of the state and the nation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(2): In the implementation of all policies, programs, and responsibilities adopted in accordance with this public education code, the Legislature, the state board, local school boards, and charter school governing boards shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(2)(a): respect, protect, and further the interests of parents in their children's public education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-201(2)(b): promote and encourage full and active participation and involvement of parents at all public schools.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-202 Planning for Utah's public education system.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
The state board shall:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-202(1): create, maintain, and review on a regular basis a statewide, comprehensive multi-year strategic plan that includes long-term goals for improved student outcomes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-202(2): (1) report annually to the Education Interim Committee on or before the committee's November meeting on the strategic plan described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301 Public education's vision and mission.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(1): The Legislature envisions an educated citizenry that encompasses the following foundational principles:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(1)(a): citizen participation in civic and political affairs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(1)(b): economic prosperity for the state by graduating students who are college and career ready;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(1)(c): strong moral and social values; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(1)(d): loyalty and commitment to constitutional government.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2): The Legislature recognizes that public education's mission is to assure Utah the best educated citizenry in the world and each individual the training to succeed in a global society by providing students with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(a): learning and occupational skills;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(b): character development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(c): literacy and numeracy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(d): high quality instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(e): curriculum based on high standards and relevance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(2)(f): effective assessment to inform high quality instruction and accountability.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(3): (2) The Legislature:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(3)(a): recognizes that parents are a child's first teachers and are responsible for the education of their children;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(3)(b): encourages family engagement and adequate preparation so that students enter the public education system ready to learn; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(3)(c): (2) intends that the mission detailed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-301(4): 53G-10-204 This section will be applied consistent with Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302 Characteristics of public education system.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Legislature shall assist in maintaining a public education system that has the following characteristics:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(1): assumes that all students have the ability to learn and that each student departing the system will be prepared to achieve success in productive employment, further education, or both;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(2): provides a personalized education plan or personalized education occupation plan for each student, which involves the student, the student's parent, and school personnel in establishing the plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(3): provides students with the knowledge and skills to take responsibility for their decisions and to make appropriate choices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(4): provides opportunities for students to exhibit the capacity to learn, think, reason, and work effectively, individually and in groups;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(5): offers world-class core standards that enable students to successfully compete in a global society, and to succeed as citizens of a constitutional republic;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(6): incorporates an information retrieval system that provides students, parents, and educators with reliable, useful, and timely data on the progress of each student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(7): attracts, prepares, inducts, and retains excellent teachers for every classroom in large part through collaborative efforts among the state board, the Utah Board of Higher Education, and school districts, provides effective ongoing professional development opportunities for teachers to improve their teaching skills, and provides recognition, rewards, and compensation for their excellence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(8): empowers each school district and public school to create its own vision and plan to achieve results consistent with the objectives outlined in this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(9): uses technology to improve teaching and learning processes and for the delivery of educational services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(10): promotes ongoing research and development projects at the district and the school level that are directed at improving or enhancing public education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(11): offers a public school choice program, which gives students and their parents options to best meet the student's personalized education needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(12): emphasizes the involvement of educators, parents, business partnerships, and the community at large in the educational process by allowing them to be involved in establishing and implementing educational goals and participating in decision-making at the school site; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-302(13): emphasizes competency-based standards and progress-based assessments, including tracking and measurement systems.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303 Family participation in educational process -- Family engagement policy.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(1): The Legislature recognizes the importance of parental participation in the educational process in order for students to achieve and maintain high levels of performance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(2): It is, therefore, the policy of the state to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(2)(a): encourage parents to provide a home environment that values education and send their children to school prepared to learn;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(2)(b): rely upon school districts and schools to provide opportunities for parents of students to be involved in establishing and implementing educational goals for their respective schools and students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(2)(c): expect employers to recognize the need for parents and members of the community to participate in the public education system in order to help students achieve and maintain excellence.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3): (3)(b)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(a): Each local school board shall adopt a policy on parental involvement in the schools of the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(b): (3)(b)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(b)(i): The local school board shall design its policy to build consistent and effective communication among parents, teachers, and administrators.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(b)(ii): (3)(b)(i) The policy described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(b)(ii)(A): shall include parents or family, when appropriate, of children learning English, regardless of prevalence of children learning English in the geographic area in which the LEA is located; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(b)(ii)(B): may include assistance from community organizations to assist through a preferred method of communication.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(c): The policy shall provide parents with the opportunity to be actively involved in their children's education and to be informed of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(c)(i): the importance of the involvement of parents in directly affecting the success of their children's educational efforts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-303(3)(c)(ii): groups and organizations that may provide instruction and training to parents to help improve their children's academic success and support their academic efforts.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304 School district and individual school powers -- Plan for college and career readiness definition.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(1): 53E-2-302 In order to acquire and develop the characteristics listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2): 53F-2-102
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a): Each school district and public school shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(i): develop and implement programs integrating technology into the curriculum, instruction, and student assessment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(ii): provide for teacher and parent involvement in policymaking at the school site;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(iii): implement a public school choice program to give parents, students, and teachers greater flexibility in designing and choosing among programs with different focuses through schools within the same district and other districts, subject to space availability, demographics, and legal and performance criteria;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(iv): establish strategic planning at both the district and school level and site-based decision making programs at the school level;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(v): provide opportunities for each student to acquire and develop academic and occupational knowledge, skills, and abilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(vi): participate in ongoing research and development projects primarily at the school level aimed at improving the quality of education within the system; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(a)(vii): involve business and industry in the education process through the establishment of partnerships with the business community at the district and school level.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b): 53F-2-102
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(i): As used in this section, "plan for college and career readiness" means a plan developed by a student and the student's parent, in consultation with school counselors, teachers, and administrators that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(i)(A): is initiated at the beginning of grade 7;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(i)(B): identifies a student's skills and objectives;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(i)(C): maps out a strategy to guide a student's course selection; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(i)(D): links a student to post-secondary options, including higher education and careers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(ii): Each local school board, in consultation with school personnel, parents, and school community councils or similar entities shall establish policies to provide for the effective implementation of an individual learning plan or a plan for college and career readiness for each student at the school site.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(iii): The policies shall include guidelines and expectations for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(iii)(A): recognizing the student's accomplishments, strengths, and progress toward meeting student achievement standards as defined in the core standards for Utah public schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(iii)(B): planning, monitoring, and managing education and career development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(iii)(C): involving students, parents, and school personnel in preparing and implementing an individual learning plan and a plan for college and career readiness.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(iv): A parent may request a conference with school personnel in addition to an individual learning plan or a plan for college and career readiness conference established by local school board policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(2)(b)(v): 53F-2-102 Time spent during the school day to implement an individual learning plan or a plan for college and career readiness is considered part of the school term  described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(3): 53E-2-302 A school district or public school may submit proposals to modify or waive rules or policies of a supervisory authority within the public education system in order to acquire or develop the characteristics listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(4)(a): Each school district and public school shall make an annual report to its patrons on its activities under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-2-304(4)(b): The reporting process shall involve participation from teachers, parents, and the community at large in determining how well the district or school is performing.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 3 - State Board of Education Organization, Powers, and Duties
*******************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "State Board of Education Organization, Powers, and Duties."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201 State board members -- Election and appointment of officers -- Removal from office.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(1): Title 20A, Chapter 14, Nomination and Election of State and Local School Boards Members of the state board shall be nominated and elected as provided in
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(2): The state board shall elect from its members a chair, and at least one vice chair, but no more than three vice chairs, every other year at a meeting held any time between November 15 and January 15.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(3)(a): If the election of officers is held subsequent to the election of a new member of the state board, but prior to the time that the new member takes office, the new member shall assume the position of the outgoing member for purposes of the election of officers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(3)(b): In all other matters the outgoing member shall retain the full authority of the office until replaced as provided by law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(4): The duties of these officers shall be determined by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(5): The state board shall appoint a secretary who serves at the pleasure of the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-201(6): An officer appointed or elected by the state board under this section may be removed from office for cause by a vote of two-thirds of the state board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-203 State board meetings -- Quorum requirements.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-203(1): The state board shall meet at the call of the chairman and at least 11 times each year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-203(2): A majority of all members is required to validate an act of the state board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-204 Gross neglect of duty -- Nonpayment of salary or expenses.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-204(1): Failure of a member of the state board or of an LEA governing board to carry out responsibilities assigned by law or to comply with rules of the state board is gross neglect of duty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-204(2): Salary or expenses shall not be paid for work which violates rules of the state board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301 Appointment -- Qualifications -- Duties.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(1)(a): The state board shall appoint a state superintendent of public instruction, who is the executive officer of the state board and serves at the pleasure of the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(1)(b): The state board shall appoint the state superintendent on the basis of outstanding professional qualifications.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(1)(c): The state superintendent shall administer all programs assigned to the state board in accordance with the policies and the standards established by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2): The state board shall, with the state superintendent, develop a statewide education strategy focusing on core academics, including the development of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(a): core standards for Utah public schools and graduation requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(b): a process to select model instructional materials that best correlate with the core standards for Utah public schools and graduation requirements that are supported by generally accepted scientific standards of evidence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(c): professional development programs for teachers, superintendents, and principals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(d): model remediation programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(e): a model method for creating individual student learning targets, and a method of measuring an individual student's performance toward those targets;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(f): progress-based assessments for ongoing performance evaluations of school districts and schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(g): incentives to achieve the desired outcome of individual student progress in core academics that do not create disincentives for setting high goals for the students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(h): an annual report card for school and school district performance, measuring learning and reporting progress-based assessments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(i): a systematic method to encourage innovation in schools and school districts as each strives to achieve improvement in performance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(2)(j): a method for identifying and sharing best demonstrated practices across school  districts and schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3): (3)(d); Part 8, Implementing Federal or National Education Programs The state superintendent shall perform duties assigned by the state board, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(a): investigating all matters pertaining to the public schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(b): adopting and keeping an official seal to authenticate the state superintendent's official acts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(c): holding and conducting meetings, seminars, and conferences on educational topics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d): (3)(d) collecting and organizing education data into an automated decision support system to facilitate school district and school improvement planning, accountability reporting, performance recognition, and the evaluation of educational policy and program effectiveness to include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(i): data that are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(i)(A): comparable across schools and school districts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(i)(B): appropriate for use in longitudinal studies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(i)(C): comprehensive with regard to the data elements required under applicable state or federal law or state board rule;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(ii): features that enable users, most particularly school administrators, teachers, and parents, to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(ii)(A): retrieve school and school district level data electronically;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(ii)(B): interpret the data visually; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(ii)(C): draw conclusions that are statistically valid; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii): (3)(d) procedures for the collection and management of education data that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(A): require the state superintendent to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(A)(I): collaborate with school districts and charter schools in designing and implementing uniform data standards and definitions;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(A)(II): undertake or sponsor research to implement improved methods for analyzing education data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(A)(III): provide for data security to prevent unauthorized access to or contamination of the data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(A)(IV): protect the confidentiality of data under state and federal privacy laws; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(d)(iii)(B): (3)(d) require all school districts and schools to comply with the data collection and management procedures established under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(e): Part 8, Implementing Federal or National Education Programs administering and implementing federal educational programs in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(3)(f): with the approval of the state board, preparing and submitting to the governor a budget for the state board to be included in the budget that the governor submits to the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(4): 53F-9-401; 53F-9-401 The state superintendent shall distribute funds deposited in the Autism Awareness Restricted Account created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-301(5): Upon leaving office, the state superintendent shall deliver to the state superintendent's successor all books, records, documents, maps, reports, papers, and other articles pertaining to the state superintendent's office.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302 Compensation of state superintendent -- Other state board employees.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302(1): The state board shall establish the compensation of the state superintendent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302(2): The state board may, as necessary for the proper administration and supervision of the public school system:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302(2)(a): appoint other employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302(2)(b): delegate appropriate duties and responsibilities to state board employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-302(3): The compensation and duties of state board employees shall be established by the state board and paid from money appropriated for that purpose.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-303 Advice by state superintendent -- Written opinions.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-303(1): The state superintendent shall advise superintendents, LEA governing boards, and other school officers upon all matters involving the welfare of the schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-303(2): The state superintendent shall, when requested by district superintendents or other school officers, provide written opinions on questions of public education, administrative policy, and procedure, but not upon questions of law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-303(3): Upon request by the state superintendent, the attorney general shall issue written opinions on questions of law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-303(4): Opinions issued under this section shall be considered to be correct and final unless set aside by a court of competent jurisdiction or by subsequent legislation.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-402 Acceptance of gifts, endowments, devises, and bequests.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-402(1): The state board, on its own behalf or on behalf of an educational institution for which the state board is the direct governing body, may accept private grants, loans, gifts, endowments, devises, or bequests which are made for educational purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-402(2): These contributions are not subject to appropriation by the Legislature.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502 State Board of Education assistance to districts and schools.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
In order to assist school districts and individual schools in acquiring and maintaining the characteristics set forth in SectionUtah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(1): provide the framework for an education system, including core competency standards and their assessment, in which school districts and public schools permit students to advance by demonstrating competency in subject matter and mastery of skills;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(2): conduct a statewide public awareness program on competency-based educational systems;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(3): compile and publish, for the state as a whole, a set of educational performance indicators describing trends in student performance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(4): promote a public education climate of high expectations and academic excellence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(5): 53E-2-302(7); 53E-6-103(2)(a); (b) disseminate successful site-based decision-making models to districts and schools and provide teacher professional development opportunities and evaluation programs for site-based plans consistent with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(6): 53E-2-301 provide a mechanism for widespread dissemination of information about strategic planning for public education, including involvement of business and industry in the education process, in order to ensure the understanding and support of all the individuals and groups concerned with the mission of public education as outlined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(7): provide for a research and development clearing house at the state level to receive and share with school districts and public schools information on effective and innovative practices and programs in education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(8): 53E-2-302(7); 53E-6-103(2)(a); (b) help school districts develop and implement guidelines, strategies, and professional development programs for administrators and teachers consistent with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-502(9): in concert with the Utah Board of Higher Education and the state's colleges of education review and revise teacher licensing requirements to be consistent with teacher preparation for participation in personalized education programs within the public schools.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-504 Child literacy program -- Coordinated activities.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-504(1): The state board, through the state superintendent, shall provide for a public service campaign to educate parents on the importance of providing their children with opportunities to develop emerging literacy skills through a statewide "Read to Me" program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-504(2): The state board shall coordinate its activities under this section with other state and community entities that are engaged in child literacy programs in order to maximize its efforts and resources, including the Utah Commission on National and Community Service.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505 Financial and economic literacy education.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1): (1)(b); (3) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(a): (1)(b) "Financial and economic activities" include activities related to the topics listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b): "Financial and economic literacy concepts" include concepts related to the following topics:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(i): basic budgeting;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(ii): saving and financial investments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(iii): banking and financial services, including balancing a checkbook or a bank account and online banking services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(iv): career management, including earning an income;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(v): rights and responsibilities of renting or buying a home;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(vi): retirement planning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(vii): loans and borrowing money, including interest, credit card debt, predatory lending, and payday loans;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(viii): insurance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(ix): federal, state, and local taxes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(x): charitable giving;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xi): identity fraud and theft;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xii): negative financial consequences of gambling;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xiii): bankruptcy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xiv): economic systems, including a description of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xiv)(A): a command system such as socialism or communism, a market system such as capitalism, and a mixed system; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xiv)(B): historic and current examples of the effects of each economic system on economic growth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xv): supply and demand;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xvi): monetary and fiscal policy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xvii): effective business plan creation, including using economic analysis in creating a plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xviii): scarcity and choices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xix): opportunity cost and tradeoffs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xx): productivity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xxi): entrepreneurism; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(b)(xxii): economic reasoning.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(1)(c): (3) "General financial literacy course" means the course of instruction administered by the state board under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a): more fully integrate existing and new financial and economic literacy education into instruction in kindergarten through grade 12 by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(i): coordinating financial and economic literacy instruction with existing instruction in other areas of the core standards for Utah public schools, such as mathematics and social studies;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(ii): using curriculum mapping;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(iii): creating training materials and staff development programs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(iii)(A): highlight areas of potential coordination between financial and economic literacy education and other core standards for Utah public schools concepts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(iii)(B): demonstrate specific examples of financial and economic literacy concepts as a way of teaching other core standards for Utah public schools concepts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(a)(iv): using appropriate financial and economic literacy assessments to improve financial and economic literacy education and, if necessary, developing assessments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b): work with interested public, private, and nonprofit entities to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b)(i): identify, and make available to teachers, online resources for financial and economic literacy education, including modules with interactive activities and turnkey instructor resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b)(ii): coordinate school use of existing financial and economic literacy education resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b)(iii): develop simple, clear, and consistent messaging to reinforce and link existing financial literacy resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b)(iv): coordinate the efforts of school, work, private, nonprofit, and other financial education providers in implementing methods of appropriately communicating to teachers, students, and parents key financial and economic literacy messages; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(b)(v): encourage parents and students to establish higher education savings, including a Utah Educational Savings Plan account;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(c): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(d): in cooperation with school districts, charter schools, and interested private and nonprofit entities, provide opportunities for professional development in financial and economic literacy concepts to teachers, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(d)(i): a statewide learning community for financial and economic literacy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(d)(ii): summer workshops; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(2)(d)(iii): online videos of experts in the field of financial and economic literacy education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3): 53E-10-301 The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(a): administer a general financial literacy course in the same manner that the state board administers other core standards for Utah public school courses for grades 9 through 12;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(b): 53E-10-301 adopt standards and objectives for the general financial literacy course that address:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(b)(i): financial and economic literacy concepts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(b)(ii): the costs of going to college, student loans, scholarships, and the Free Application for Federal Student Aid;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(b)(iii): 53E-10-301 financial benefits of pursuing concurrent enrollment as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(b)(iv): technology that relates to banking, savings, and financial products; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c)(i): contract with a provider, through a request for proposals process, to develop an online, end-of-course assessment for the general financial literacy course;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c)(ii): require a school district or charter school to administer an online, end-of-course assessment to a student who takes the general financial literacy course; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c)(iii): develop a plan, through the state superintendent, to analyze the results of an online, end-of-course assessment in general financial literacy that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c)(iii)(A): an analysis of assessment results by standard; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(3)(c)(iii)(B): average scores statewide and by school district and school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(a): The state board shall establish a task force to study and make recommendations to the state board on how to improve financial and economic literacy education in the public school system.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(b): The task force membership shall include representatives of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(b)(i): the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(b)(ii): school districts and charter schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(b)(iii): the Utah Board of Higher Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(b)(iv): private or public entities that teach financial education and share a commitment to empower individuals and families to achieve economic stability, opportunity, and upward mobility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-505(4)(c): The state board shall convene the task force at least once every three years to review and recommend adjustments to the standards and objectives of the general financial literacy course.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506 Educational program on the use of information technology.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(1): The state board shall provide for an educational program on the use of information technology, which shall be offered by high schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2): An educational program on the use of information technology shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(a): provide instruction on skills and competencies essential for the workplace and requested by employers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b): include the following components:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(i): a curriculum;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(ii): online access to the curriculum;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(iii): instructional software for classroom and student use;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(iv): certification of skills and competencies most frequently requested by employers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(v): professional development for teachers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(b)(vi): deployment and program support, including integration with existing core standards for Utah public schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-506(2)(c): be made available to high school students, faculty, and staff.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(3): shall cooperate with federal and state governments to administer programs that promote and maintain career and technical education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(4): 53B-2a-201; 53B-2a-201 shall cooperate with the Utah Board of Higher Education, technical colleges, and degree-granting institutions that provide technical education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(5): shall require that before a minor student may participate in clinical experiences as part of a health care occupation program at a high school or other institution to which the student has been referred, the student's parent has:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(5)(a): been first given written notice through appropriate disclosure when registering and prior to participation that the program contains a clinical experience segment in which the student will observe and perform specific health care procedures that may include personal care, patient bathing, and bathroom assistance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(5)(b): provided specific written consent for the student's participation in the program and clinical experience;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-507(6): 53B-2a-201; 53E-1-203; 53B-2a-201 shall, after consulting with school districts, charter schools, the Utah Board of Higher Education, technical colleges, and degree-granting institutions that provide technical education described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509 Gang prevention and intervention policies.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(1)(a): The state board shall adopt rules that require a local school board or charter school governing board to enact gang prevention and intervention policies for all schools within the state board's jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(1)(b): (1)(a) The rules described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2): (1); (2)(f)(i); (iv) The rules described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(a): school faculty and personnel shall report suspected gang activities relating to the school and its students to a school administrator and law enforcement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(b): a student who participates in gang activities may be excluded from participation in extracurricular activities, including interscholastic athletics, as determined by the school administration after consultation with law enforcement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(c): gang-related graffiti or damage to school property shall result in parent notification and appropriate administrative and law enforcement actions, which may include obtaining restitution from those responsible for the damage;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(d): if a serious gang-related incident, as determined by the school administrator in consultation with local law enforcement, occurs on school property, at school related activities, or on a site that is normally considered to be under school control, notification shall be provided to parents of students in the school:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(d)(i): informing them, in general terms, about the incident, but removing all personally identifiable information about students from the notice;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(d)(ii): emphasizing the school's concern for safety; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(d)(iii): outlining the action taken at the school regarding the incident;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(e): school faculty and personnel shall be trained by experienced evidence based trainers that may include community gang specialists and law enforcement as part of comprehensive strategies to recognize early warning signs for youth in trouble and help students resist serious involvement in undesirable activity, including joining gangs or mimicking gang behavior;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f): (2)(f)(i); (iv) prohibitions on the following behavior:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(i): advocating or promoting a gang or any gang-related activities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(ii): marking school property, books, or school work with gang names, slogans, or signs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(iii): conducting gang initiations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(iv): threatening another person with bodily injury or inflicting bodily injury on another in connection with a gang or gang-related activity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(v): (2)(f)(i); (iv) aiding or abetting an activity described under Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(vi): displaying or wearing common gang apparel, common dress, or identifying signs or symbols on one's clothing, person, or personal property that is disruptive to the school environment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(2)(f)(vii): communicating in any method, including verbal, non-verbal, and electronic means, designed to convey gang membership or affiliation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(3): (1); (1) The rules described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-509(4): (1) The state board may consult with appropriate committees, including committees that provide opportunities for the input of parents, law enforcement, and community agencies, as it develops, enacts, and administers the rules described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510 Control of school meals program revenues -- Apportionment -- Costs.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(1)(a): School meals program revenues shall be under the control of the state board and may only be disbursed, transferred, or drawn upon by the state board's order.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(1)(b): The school meals program revenues may only be used to provide school meals and a school meals program in the state's LEAs in accordance with standards established by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(2)(a): The state board shall apportion the school meals program revenues according to the number of school children receiving school meals in each LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(2)(b): The state board and LEA governing boards shall employ staff to administer and supervise the school meals program and purchase supplies and equipment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-510(3): The costs of the school meals program shall be included in the state board's annual budget.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-601 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-602 Auditors appointed -- Auditing standards.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-602(1): Procedures utilized by auditors employed by local school boards shall meet or exceed generally accepted auditing standards approved by the state board and the state auditor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-602(2): The standards must include financial accounting for both revenue and expenditures, and student accounting.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-603 State board to verify audits.
-------------------------------------------------------------
The state board is responsible for verifying audits of financial and student accounting records of school districts for purposes of determining the allocation of Uniform School Fund money.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-701 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702 State board to adopt public school construction guidelines.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(1): As used in this section, "public school construction" means construction work on a new public school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(2): (2)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(2)(a): The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(2)(a)(i): adopt guidelines for public school construction; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(2)(a)(ii): consult with the Division of Facilities Construction and Management Administration on proposed guidelines before adoption.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(2)(b): (2)(a)(i) The state board shall ensure that guidelines adopted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(3): Before a school district or charter school may begin public school construction, the school district or charter school shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(3)(a): review the guidelines adopted by the state board under this section; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(3)(b): take into consideration the guidelines when planning the public school construction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(4): In adopting the guidelines for public school construction, the state board shall consider the following and adopt alternative guidelines as needed:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(4)(a): location factors, including whether the school is in a rural or urban setting, and climate factors;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(4)(b): variations in guidelines for significant or minimal projected student population growth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(4)(c): guidelines specific to schools that serve various populations and grades, including high schools, junior high schools, middle schools, elementary schools, alternative schools, and schools for people with disabilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(4)(d): year-round use.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5): The guidelines shall address the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(a): square footage per student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(b): minimum and maximum required real property for a public school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(c): athletic facilities and fields, playgrounds, and hard surface play areas;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(d): cost per square foot;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(e): minimum and maximum qualities and costs for building materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(f): design efficiency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(g): parking;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(h): furnishing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(i): proof of compliance with applicable building codes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-702(5)(j): safety.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703 Construction and alteration of schools and plants -- Advertising for bids -- Payment and performance bonds -- Contracts -- Bidding limitations on local school boards -- Interest of local school board members.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(1): As used in this section, the word "sealed" does not preclude acceptance of electronically sealed and submitted bids or proposals in addition to bids or proposals manually sealed and submitted.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(a): Prior to the construction of any school or the alteration of any existing school plant, if the total estimated accumulative building project cost exceeds $80,000, a local school board shall advertise for bids on the project at least 10 days before the bid due date.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(b): The advertisement shall state:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(b)(i): that proposals for the building project are required to be sealed in accordance with plans and specifications provided by the local school board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(b)(ii): where and when the proposals will be opened;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(b)(iii): that the local school board reserves the right to reject any and all proposals; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(b)(iv): that a person that submits a proposal is required to submit a certified check or bid bond, of not less than 5% of the bid in the proposal, to accompany the proposal.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(c): The local school board shall publish the advertisement, at a minimum:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(c)(i): on the local school board's website; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(c)(ii): on a state website that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(c)(ii)(A): owned or managed by, or provided under contract with, the Division of Purchasing and General Services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(2)(c)(ii)(B): available for the posting of public procurement notices.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3)(a): The local school board shall meet at the time and place specified in the advertisement and publicly open and read all received proposals.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3)(b): If satisfactory bids are received, the local school board shall award the contract to the lowest responsible bidder.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3)(c): If none of the proposals are satisfactory, all shall be rejected.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3)(d): The local school board shall again advertise in the manner provided in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(3)(e): If, after advertising a second time no satisfactory bid is received, the local school board may proceed under its own direction with the required project.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(4): (2)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(4)(a): (2)(b) The check or bond required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(4)(b): If the successful bidder fails or refuses to enter into the contract and furnish the additional bonds required under this section, then the bidder's check or bond is forfeited to the district.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(5): 63G-6a-1103 A local school board shall require payment and performance bonds of the successful bidder as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(6)(a): A local school board may require in the proposed contract that up to 5% of the contract price be withheld until the project is completed and accepted by the local school board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(6)(b): If money is withheld, the local school board shall place it in an interest bearing account, and the interest accrues for the benefit of the contractor and subcontractors.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(6)(c): This money shall be paid upon completion of the project and acceptance by the local school board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(7)(a): A local school board may not bid on projects within the district if the total accumulative estimated cost exceeds $80,000.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(7)(b): The local school board may use its resources if no satisfactory bids are received under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(8): 63G-6a-1302; Title 63G, Chapter 6a, Utah Procurement Code If the local school board determines in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-703(9): A local school board member may not have a direct or indirect financial interest in the construction project contract.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-704 Restrictions on local school district procurement of architect-engineer services.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-704(1): 58-3a-102; 58-22-102 As used in this section, "architect-engineer services" means those professional services within the scope of the practice of architecture as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-704(2): When a local school district elects to obtain architect or engineering services by using a competitive procurement process and has provided public notice of its competitive procurement process:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-704(2)(a): a higher education entity, or any part of one, may not submit a proposal in response to the state agency's competitive procurement process; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-704(2)(b): the local school district may not award a contract to perform the architect or engineering services solicited in the competitive procurement process to a higher education entity or any part of one.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-705 School plant capital outlay report.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-705(1): The state board shall prepare an annual school plant capital outlay report of all school districts, which includes information on the number and size of building projects completed and under construction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-705(2): A school district or charter school shall prepare and submit an annual school plant capital outlay report to the state auditor on or before a date designated by the state auditor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(a)(iv)(D): (3)(a)(iv)(C)(I)(Bb) Upon the local school board or charter school remedying the deficiencies indicated in the notice under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(a)(iv)(E): (3)(a)(iv)(E)(I)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(a)(iv)(E)(I): The state superintendent may charge the school district or charter school a fee for an inspection that the state superintendent considers necessary to enable the state superintendent to issue a certificate authorizing permanent occupancy of the school building.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(a)(iv)(E)(II): (3)(a)(iv)(E)(I) A fee under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(b): (3) For purposes of this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(b)(i): "local governmental entity" means either a municipality, for a school building located within a municipality, or a county, for a school building located within an unincorporated area in the county; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-706(3)(b)(ii): "certificate of inspection verification" means a standard inspection form developed by the state superintendent in consultation with local school boards and charter schools to verify that inspections by qualified inspectors have occurred.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707 School building construction and inspection manual -- Annual construction and inspection conference -- Verification of school construction inspections.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(1)(a): The state board, through the state superintendent, shall develop and distribute to each school district a school building construction and inspection resource manual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(1)(b): The manual shall be provided to a charter school upon request of the charter school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(2): 53E-3-702
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(2)(a): 53E-3-702 The manual shall include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(2)(a)(i): current legal requirements; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(2)(a)(ii): 53E-3-702 information on school building construction and inspections, including the guidelines adopted by the state board in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(3)(a): receive current information on the design, construction, and inspection of school buildings;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(3)(b)(iv): adequate documentation of school building inspections; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(3)(c): provide input on any changes that may be needed to improve the existing school building inspection program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-707(4): The state board shall develop a process to verify that inspections by qualified inspectors occur in each school district or charter school.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-708 Licensed architect to prepare plans.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
A licensed architect shall prepare the plans and specifications for the construction or alteration of school buildings.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-709 Power of state board regarding expected federal aid to build schools.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
For the purpose of participating in any program of assistance by the government of the United States designed to aid the various states, their political subdivisions and their educational agencies and institutions in providing adequate educational buildings and facilities, the state board, with the approval of the governor, may do the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-709(1): It may develop and implement plans relating to the building of educational buildings for the use and benefit of school districts and educational institutions and agencies of the state.  These plans may conform to the requirements of federal legislation to such extent as the state board finds necessary to qualify the state and its educational subdivisions, agencies, and institutions for federal educational building grants-in-aid.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-709(2): It may enter into agreements on behalf of the state, its school districts, and its educational agencies and institutions with the federal government and its agencies, and with the school districts, educational agencies, and institutions of the state, as necessary to comply with federal legislation and to secure for them rights of participation as necessary to fulfill the educational building needs of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-3-709(3): It may accept, allocate, disburse, and otherwise deal with federal funds or other assets that are available for buildings from any federal legislation or program of assistance among the school districts, public educational agencies, and other public institutions eligible to participate in those programs.
