Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307 Benchmark assessments in reading -- Report to parent.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(1): 53G-11-303; 53G-11-303 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(1)(a): "Competency" means a demonstrable acquisition of a specified knowledge, skill, or ability that has been organized into a hierarchical arrangement leading to higher levels of knowledge, skill, or ability.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(1)(b): "Diagnostic assessment" means an assessment that measures key literacy skills, including phonemic awareness, sound-symbol recognition, alphabet knowledge, decoding and encoding skills, and comprehension, to determine a student's specific strengths and weaknesses in a skill area.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(1)(c): 53G-11-303 "Evidence-based" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(1)(d): 53G-11-303 "Evidence-informed" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(2): The state board shall approve a benchmark assessment for use statewide by school districts and charter schools to assess the reading competency of students in grades 1 through 6 as provided by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(3): A school district or charter school shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(3)(a): administer benchmark assessments to students in grades 1, 2, and 3 at the beginning, middle, and end of the school year using the benchmark assessment approved by the state board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(3)(b): after administering a benchmark assessment, report the results to a student's parent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4): 53F-4-203; 53G-11-303; 53G-11-303(1)(a); (4)(a)(vi)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a): If a benchmark assessment or supplemental reading assessment indicates a student lacks competency in a reading skill, or is lagging behind other students in the student's grade in acquiring a reading skill, the school district or charter school shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(i): administer diagnostic assessments to the student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(ii): using data from the diagnostic assessment, provide specific, focused, and individualized intervention or tutoring to develop the reading skill;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(iii): administer formative assessments and progress monitoring at recommended levels for the benchmark assessment to measure the success of the focused intervention;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(iv): inform the student's parent of activities that the parent may engage in with the student to assist the student in improving reading proficiency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(v): provide information to the parent regarding appropriate interventions available to the student outside of the regular school day that may include tutoring, before and after school programs, or summer school; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(a)(vi): provide instructional materials that are evidence-informed for core instruction and evidence-based for intervention and supplemental instruction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307(4)(b): 53F-4-203; 53G-11-303; 53G-11-303(1)(a); (4)(a)(vi) Nothing in this section or in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5 Mathematics benchmark assessment.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(1): As used in this section, "early mathematics benchmark assessment" or "benchmark assessment" means a standardized assessment to measure the acquisition of mathematics skills in kindergarten and grades 1 through 3 that includes predictive indicators of academic achievement based on measures of early mathematics, computation, and problem solving.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(2): The state board may approve a benchmark assessment for use statewide by LEAs to assess the mathematics competency of students in kindergarten and grades 1 through 3.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(3): (2); (3)(a) If the state board approves a benchmark assessment for statewide use under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(3)(a): administer benchmark assessments to students at the beginning, middle, and end of the school year using the mathematics benchmark assessment in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(3)(a)(i): kindergarten, as an optional assessment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(3)(a)(ii): grades 1 through 3, as a required assessment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(3)(b): (3)(a) after administering a benchmark assessment described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(4): (2) In making the approval described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(4)(a): prioritize the assessment's reliability, validity, speed, and efficiency; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(4)(b): ensure the mathematics benchmark assessment's ability to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(4)(b)(i): identify students who may be at risk for mathematics difficulties; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-307.5(4)(b)(ii): measure students' progress through data.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308 Unique student identifier -- Coordination of higher education and public education information technology systems -- Coordination of preschool and public education information technology systems.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(1): As used in this section, "unique student identifier" means an alphanumeric code assigned to each public education student for identification purposes, which:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(1)(a): is not assigned to any former or current student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(1)(b): does not incorporate personal information, including a birth date or Social Security number.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(2): The state board, through the state superintendent, shall assign each public education student a unique student identifier, which shall be used to track individual student performance on achievement tests administered under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(3): 53B-33-201; 53B-1-109 The state board and the Utah Board of Higher Education, in collaboration with the Utah Data Research Center created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(3)(a): 53B-1-109 coordinate public education and higher education information technology systems to allow individual student academic achievement to be tracked through both education systems in accordance with this section and Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-308(3)(b): coordinate access to the unique student identifier of a public education student who later attends an institution within the state system of higher education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-309 Grade level specification change.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-309(1): The state board may change a grade level specification for the administration of specific assessments under this part to a different grade level specification or a competency-based specification if the specification is more consistent with patterns of school organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-309(2): (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-309(2)(a): (1) If the state board changes a grade level specification described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-309(2)(b): The state board shall submit the report at least six months before the anticipated change.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310 Scoring -- Reports of results.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(1): For a statewide assessment that requires the use of a student answer sheet, a local school board or charter school governing board shall submit all answer sheets on a per-school and per-class basis to the state superintendent for scoring unless the assessment requires scoring by a national testing service.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(2): The district, school, and class results of the statewide assessments, but not the score or relative position of individual students, shall be reported to each local school board or charter school governing board annually at a regularly scheduled meeting.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(3): A local school board or charter school governing board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(3)(a): shall make copies of the report available to the general public upon request; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(3)(b): may charge a fee for the cost of copying the report.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(4)(a): The state board shall annually provide to school districts and charter schools a comprehensive report for each of the school district's and charter school's students showing the student's statewide assessment results for each year that the student took a statewide assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-310(4)(b): A school district or charter school shall give a copy of the comprehensive report to the student's parents and make the report available to school staff, as appropriate.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311 Analysis of results -- Staff professional development.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(1): The state board, through the state superintendent, shall develop an online data reporting tool to analyze the results of statewide assessments.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2): The online data reporting tool shall include components designed to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2)(a): assist school districts and individual schools to use the results of the analysis in planning, evaluating, and enhancing programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2)(b): identify schools not achieving state-established acceptable levels of student performance in order to assist those schools in improving student performance levels; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2)(c): provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2)(c)(i): for statistical reporting of statewide assessment results at state, school district, school, and grade or course levels; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(2)(c)(ii): actual levels of performance on statewide assessments.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(3): A local school board or charter school governing board shall provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(3)(a): evaluation of the statewide assessment results and use of the evaluations in setting goals and establishing programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(3)(b): a professional development program that provides teachers, principals, and other professional staff with the training required to successfully establish and maintain statewide assessments.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-311(4): (2)(b) The state board is not required to identify schools not achieving state-established acceptable levels of student performance as described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-312 Preparation for tests.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-312(1): School district employees may not conduct any specific instruction or preparation of students that would be a breach of testing ethics, such as the teaching of specific test questions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-312(2): School district employees who administer the test shall follow the standardization procedures in the test administration manual for an assessment and any additional specific instructions developed by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-312(3): The state board may revoke the certification of an individual who violates this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-313 Construction of part.
-----------------------------------------------------
Nothing in this part shall be construed to mean or represented to require that graduation from a high school or promotion to another grade is in any way dependent upon successful performance of any test administered as a part of the testing program established under this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-315 Waiver of requirement to administer certain assessments.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-315(1): A statutory requirement to administer an assessment with which an LEA or the state board has not fully complied at the time of statewide school closures beginning on March 16, 2020, is waived for the 2019-20 school year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-315(2): Nothing in this section prohibits an LEA or the state board from administering an assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-315(3): This section supersedes any conflicting provisions of Utah law.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "instructional materials" means textbooks or materials used as, or in place of, textbooks and which may be used within the state curriculum framework for courses of study by students in public schools, including:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401(1): textbooks;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401(2): workbooks;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401(3): computer software;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401(4): online or Internet courses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-401(5): audio and video media.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402 Creation of commission -- Powers -- Payment of expenses.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1): The state board shall appoint a State Instructional Materials Commission consisting of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(a): the state superintendent or the state superintendent's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(b): a school district superintendent;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(c): a secondary school principal;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(d): an elementary school principal;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(e): a secondary school teacher;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(f): an elementary school teacher;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(g): five persons not employed in public education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(1)(h): a dean of a school of education of a state college or university.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(2): The commission shall evaluate instructional materials for recommendation by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-402(3): Members shall serve without compensation, but their actual and necessary expenses incurred in the performance of their official duties shall be paid out of money appropriated to the state board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403 Commission's evaluation of instructional materials -- Recommendation by the state board.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(1): Semi-annually after reviewing the evaluations of the commission, the state board shall recommend instructional materials for use in the public schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(2): The standard period of time instructional materials shall remain on the list of recommended instructional materials shall be five years.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(3): Unsatisfactory instructional materials may be removed from the list of recommended instructional materials at any time within the period applicable to the instructional materials.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(4): 53G-10-103; 53G-10-402 Except as provided in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(4)(a): instructional materials recommended by the state board as provided in this section; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-403(4)(b): other instructional materials the school considers appropriate to teach the core standards for Utah public schools.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-404 Meetings -- Notice.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-404(1): The commission shall meet at the call of the state superintendent or the state superintendent's designee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-404(2): 52-4-202 Notice of a meeting shall be given as required under Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405 Sealed proposals for instructional materials contracts -- Sample copies -- Price of instructional materials.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405(1): As used in this section, the word "sealed" does not preclude acceptance of electronically sealed and submitted bids or proposals in addition to bids or proposals manually sealed and submitted.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405(2): A person seeking a contract to furnish instructional materials for use in the public schools shall submit a sealed proposal to the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405(3): Each proposal must:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405(3)(a): be accompanied by sample copies of the instructional materials to be reviewed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-405(3)(b): include the wholesale price at which the publisher agrees to furnish the instructional materials to districts and schools during the approval period.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-406 Awarding instructional materials contracts.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-406(1): The state board shall award contracts for furnishing instructional materials.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-406(2): If a satisfactory proposal to furnish instructional materials is not received, a new request for proposals may be issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-4-407 Illegal acts -- Misdemeanor.
------------------------------------------------------------
It is a class B misdemeanor for a member of the commission or the state board to receive money or other remuneration as an inducement for the recommendation or introduction of instructional materials into the schools.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Accountability."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201(1): "Lowest performing 25% of students" means the proportion of a school's students who scored in the lowest 25% of students in the school on a statewide assessment based on the prior school year's scores.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201(2): 53E-4-303; 53E-4-304; 53E-4-305 "Statewide assessment" means one or more of the following, as applicable:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201(2)(a): 53E-4-303 a standards assessment described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201(2)(c): 53E-4-305 a college readiness assessment described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-201(2)(d): an alternate assessment administered to a student with a disability.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210 State board duties -- Proficient level -- Student growth -- English learner adequate progress.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(1)(a): For the purpose of determining whether a student scores at or above the proficient level on a statewide assessment, the state board shall determine, through a process that evaluates student performance based on specific criteria, the minimum level that demonstrates proficiency for each statewide assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(1)(b): (1)(a) If the state board adjusts the minimum level that demonstrates proficiency described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(2)(a): For the purpose of determining whether a student's performance on a statewide assessment is equal to or exceeds the student's academic growth target, the state board shall calculate, for each individual student, the amount of growth necessary to achieve or maintain proficiency by a future school year determined by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(2)(b): For the purpose of determining the amount of a student's growth on a statewide assessment compared to other students with similar prior assessment scores, the state board shall calculate growth as a percentile for a student using appropriate statistical methods.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-210(3): For the purpose of determining whether an English learner achieves adequate progress on an English learner assessment established by the state board, the state board shall determine the minimum progress that demonstrates adequate progress.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(1): 53G-5-102 "Charter school authorizer" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(2): "Cohort" means all district schools and charter schools identified as:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(2)(a): springboard schools based on school accountability results from the same school year; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(2)(b): elevate schools based on school accountability results from the same school year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(3): 53E-5-305 "Continuous improvement expert" means a person identified by the state board under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(4): 53E-6-102 "Educator" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(5): 53E-5-302.1 "Elevate school" means a district school or charter school that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(5)(a): is not a Title I school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(5)(b): is implementing targeted support and improvement activities under 20 U.S.C. Sec. 6311; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(5)(c): 53E-5-302.1 has applied and been designated by the state board as an elevate school as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(6): "Final remedial year" means the second or third school year following the initial remedial year, as determined by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(7): 53E-5-302; 53E-5-302.1 "Initial remedial year" means the school year a district school or charter school is designated as a springboard school under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(8): "LEA governing board" means a local school board or charter school governing board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(9): Part 2, School Accountability System "School accountability system" means the school accountability system established in
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(10): 53E-5-303; 53E-5-304 "School improvement committee" means a committee established under:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(10)(a): 53E-5-303 for a district school, Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(10)(b): 53E-5-304 for a charter school, Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(11): 53E-5-303; 53E-5-304 "School improvement plan" means a plan described in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(11)(a): 53E-5-303 for a district school, Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(11)(b): 53E-5-304 for a charter school, Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(12): Title 53E, Chapter 5, Part 2, School Accountability System "Springboard school" means a district school or charter school that has been designated a springboard school by the state board because the school:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(12)(a): is not a Title I school; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(12)(b): Title 53E, Chapter 5, Part 2, School Accountability System when ranked according to the percentage of possible points the state board awards under
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(12)(b)(i): one of the five lowest performing elementary, middle, or junior high schools statewide; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-301(12)(b)(ii): one of the two lowest performing high schools statewide.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302 State board to designate springboard schools -- Needs assessment.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302(1): The state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302(1)(a): beginning in the 2025-2026 school year, and every four years thereafter, designate a school as a springboard school; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302(1)(b): conduct a needs assessment for a springboard school by thoroughly analyzing the root causes of the springboard school's performance qualifying the school for designation as a springboard school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302(2): (1)(b) The state board may use up to 5% of the appropriation provided under this part to hire or contract with one or more individuals to conduct a needs assessment described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1 State board to designate elevate schools -- Needs assessment.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1): Beginning in the 2022-2023 school year, in every year that the state board does not designate a springboard school, the state board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1)(a): accept applications to be designated an elevate school from schools that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1)(a)(i): are not Title I schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1)(a)(ii): are implementing targeted support and improvement activities under 20 U.S.C. Sec. 6311;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1)(b): identify at least six schools as elevate schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(1)(c): conduct a needs assessment for an elevate school by thoroughly analyzing the root causes of the school's previous performance of targeted support and improvement student groups.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-302.1(2): (1)(c) The state board may use up to 5% of the appropriation provided under this part to hire or contract with one or more individuals to conduct a needs assessment described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(4)(b)(iv): provide high-quality professional learning personalized for school staff that is designed to build:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(4)(b)(iv)(A): the leadership capacity of the school principal;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(4)(b)(iv)(B): the instructional capacity of school staff;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(4)(b)(v): leverage support from community partners to coordinate an efficient delivery of supports to students inside and outside the classroom;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(4)(e): may include pay for performance provisions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(5): (1); 53E-5-302 A school improvement committee shall partner with the continuous improvement expert selected under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(5)(a): 53E-5-302 addresses the root causes of the springboard school's or elevate school's low performance identified through the needs assessment described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(5)(b): includes recommendations regarding changes to the springboard school's or elevate school's personnel, culture, curriculum, assessments, instructional practices, governance, leadership, finances, policies, or other areas that may be necessary to implement the school improvement plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(5)(c): includes measurable student achievement goals and objectives and benchmarks by which to measure progress;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(6)(d)(i)(C): how the community may provide support to the school and students of the school inside and outside the classroom; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(6)(d)(ii): to:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-5-303(6)(d)(ii)(B): the governing council and the mayor of the municipality in which the school is located.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 6 - Education Professional Licensure
******************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Education Professional Licensure."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(1): "Certificate" means a license issued by a governmental jurisdiction outside the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(2): "Educator" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(2)(a): a person who holds a license;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(2)(b): a teacher, counselor, administrator, librarian, or other person required, under rules of the state board, to hold a license; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(2)(c): a person who is the subject of an allegation which has been received by the state board or UPPAC and was, at the time noted in the allegation, a license holder or a person employed in a position requiring licensure.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(3): "License" means an authorization issued by the state board that permits the holder to serve in a professional capacity in the public schools.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(4): "National Board certification" means a current certificate issued by the National Board for Professional Teaching Standards.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(5): "School" means a public or private entity that provides educational services to a minor child.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-102(6): "UPPAC" means the Utah Professional Practices Advisory Commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103 Legislative findings on teacher quality -- Declaration of education as a profession.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(1)(a): The Legislature acknowledges that education is perhaps the most important function of state and local governments, recognizing that the future success of our state and nation depend in large part upon the existence of a responsible and educated citizenry.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(1)(b): The Legislature further acknowledges that the primary responsibility for the education of children within the state resides with their parents and that the role of state and local governments is to support and assist parents in fulfilling that responsibility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(a): The Legislature finds that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(a)(i): quality teaching is the basic building block of successful schools and, outside of home and family circumstances, the essential component of student achievement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(a)(ii): the high quality of teachers is absolutely essential to enhance student achievement and to assure educational excellence in each classroom in the state's public schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(a)(iii): the implementation of a comprehensive continuum of data-driven strategies regarding recruitment, preservice, licensure, induction, professional development, and evaluation is essential if the state and its citizens expect every classroom to be staffed by a skilled, caring, and effective teacher.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(b): In providing for the safe and effective performance of the function of educating Utah's children, the Legislature further finds it to be of critical importance that education, including instruction, administrative, and supervisory services, be recognized as a profession, and that those who are licensed or seek to become licensed and to serve as educators:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(b)(i): meet high standards both as to qualifications and fitness for service as educators through quality recruitment and preservice programs before assuming their responsibilities in the schools;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(b)(ii): maintain those standards in the performance of their duties while holding licenses, in large part through participating in induction and ongoing professional development programs focused on instructional improvement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(b)(iii): receive fair, systematic evaluations of their performance at school for the purpose of enhancing the quality of public education and student achievement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-103(2)(b)(iv): have access to a process for fair examination and review of allegations made against them and for the administration of appropriate sanctions against those found, in accordance with due process, to have failed to conduct themselves in a manner commensurate with their authority and responsibility to provide appropriate professional services to the children of the state.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201 State board licensure.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; 53F-4-504; 53F-4-503; (1)(c) The state board shall establish in rule made in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1)(a): an associate educator license that permits an individual to provide educational services in a public school while working to meet the requirements of a professional educator license;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1)(b): a professional educator license that permits an individual to provide educational services in a public school after demonstrating that the individual meets licensure requirements established in state board rule;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1)(c): an LEA-specific educator license issued by the state board at the request of an LEA's governing body that is valid for an individual to provide educational services in the requesting LEA's schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1)(d): 53F-4-504; 53F-4-503; (1)(c) beginning in the 2023-2024 school year, a provider-specific license issued by the state board at the request of an authorized online course provider described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(1)(d)(i): 53F-4-503 is valid for an individual to provide educational services to a student enrolled in an online course described in

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(2): An individual employed in a position that requires licensure by the state board shall hold the license that is appropriate to the position.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(3)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board may by rule made in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(3)(b): An educator who is enrolling in a course of study at an institution within the state system of higher education to satisfy the state board requirements for retaining a license is exempt from tuition, except for a semester registration fee established by the Utah Board of Higher Education, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(3)(b)(i): the educator is enrolled on the basis of surplus space in the class after regularly enrolled students have been assigned and admitted to the class in accordance with regular procedures, normal teaching loads, and the institution's approved budget; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-201(3)(b)(ii): enrollments are determined by each institution under rules and guidelines established by the Utah Board of Higher Education in accordance with findings of fact that space is available for the educator's enrollment.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-204 Exemptions from licensure.
----------------------------------------------------------
Except as otherwise provided by statute or rule, a spouse of an individual serving in the armed forces of the United States while the individual is stationed within this state may work as an educator without being licensed under this title if:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-204(1): the spouse holds a valid educator license issued by any other state or jurisdiction recognized by the state board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-204(2): the license is current and the spouse is in good standing in the state or jurisdiction of licensure.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-301(5): (4); 53E-6-201; Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act If the state board uses a required literacy preparation assessment under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-302 Educator preparation programs.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-302(1): 53E-6-301 As used in this section:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-302(2): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-302(3): (2) The state board shall ensure that standards adopted under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-302(4): The state board shall designate an employee of the state board's staff to:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307 Certification in other jurisdictions -- Impact on licensing in Utah.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(1): An applicant for a license, renewal of a license, or reinstatement of a license shall provide the administrator of teacher licensing with an affidavit, stating under oath the current status of any certificate, license, or other authorization required for a professional position in education, which the applicant holds or has held in any other jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(2): 53G-11-405 An applicant for a license who has held a teacher's license in any other jurisdiction or who graduated from an institution of higher education in another state shall also provide the administrator of teacher licensing with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(2)(a): a complete listing of the higher education institutions attended by the applicant, whether the applicant's enrollment or eligibility for completion of a program was terminated by the institution, and, if so, the reasons for termination;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(2)(b): a complete list of prior school employers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(2)(c): 53G-11-405 a release on a form provided by the administrator permitting the state board to obtain records from other jurisdictions and from institutions of higher education attended by the applicant, including expunged or otherwise protected records, relating to any offense described substantially in the same language as in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(3): If the applicant's certificate, license, or authorization as an educator in any other jurisdiction is under investigation, has expired or been surrendered, suspended or revoked, or is currently not valid for any other reason, the state board may not grant the requested license, renewal, or reinstatement until it has received confirmation from the administrator of professional certification in that jurisdiction that the applicant would be eligible for certification or licensure in that jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-307(4): (3) The state board may not withhold a license for the sole reason that the applicant would be ineligible for certification, licensure, or authorization in the jurisdiction referred to in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-501 Utah Professional Practices Advisory Commission established.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Utah Professional Practices Advisory Commission, UPPAC, is established to assist and advise the state board in matters relating to the professional practices of educators.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502 UPPAC members -- Executive secretary.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(1): UPPAC shall consist of a nonvoting executive secretary and 11 voting members, nine of whom shall be licensed educators in good standing, and two of whom shall be members nominated by the education organization within the state that has the largest membership of parents of students and teachers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(2): Six of the voting members shall be persons whose primary responsibility is teaching.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(3): 53E-6-503
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(3)(a): The state superintendent shall appoint an employee to serve as executive secretary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(3)(b): 53E-6-503 Voting members are appointed by the state superintendent as provided under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-502(4): State board employees shall staff UPPAC activities.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503 Nominations -- Appointment of commission members -- Reappointments.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(1)(a): The state board shall adopt rules establishing procedures for nominating and appointing individuals to voting membership on UPPAC.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(1)(b): Nomination petitions must be filed with the state superintendent prior to June 16 of the year of appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(1)(c): A nominee for appointment as a member of UPPAC as an educator must have been employed in the representative class in the Utah public school system or a private school accredited by the state board during the three years immediately preceding the date of appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(2): The state superintendent shall appoint the members of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(3): Appointments begin July 1 and are for terms of three years and until a successor is appointed.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(4): Terms of office are staggered so that approximately 1/3 of UPPAC members are appointed annually.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-503(5): A member may not serve more than two terms.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-504 Filling of vacancies.
-----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-504(1): A UPPAC vacancy occurs if a member resigns, fails to attend three or more meetings during a calendar year, or no longer meets the requirements for nomination and appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-504(2): If a vacancy occurs, the state superintendent shall appoint a successor to fill the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-504(3): If the state superintendent does not fill the vacancy within 60 days, the state board shall make the appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-504(4): Nominations to fill vacancies are submitted to the state superintendent in accordance with procedures established under rules of the state board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-505 Meetings and expenses of UPPAC members.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-505(1): UPPAC shall meet at least quarterly and at the call of the chair or of a majority of the members.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-505(2): Members of UPPAC serve without compensation but are allowed reimbursement for actual and necessary expenses under the rules of the Division of Finance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-505(3): The state board shall pay reimbursement to UPPAC members out of the Income Tax Fund.

------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-506(3)(b): In conducting an investigation, UPPAC or an independent investigator shall conduct the investigation independent of and separate from a related criminal investigation.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-506(4): The state board may direct UPPAC to:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-506(5): UPPAC may not participate as a party in a dispute relating to negotiations between:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-601 Definition.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this part "hearing" means a proceeding held in accordance with generally accepted principles of due process and administrative law in which definite issues of fact or of law are tried before a hearing body, and in which proceeding evidence is presented and witnesses heard, and in which the party against whom the proceedings are held has a right to:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-601(1): appear with or without counsel to present evidence, confront and cross-examine witnesses, or subpoena witnesses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-601(2): obtain a decision based solely upon evidence presented to the hearing body in the presence of both parties or representatives of both parties, recognizing that presence is satisfied if a party has been given a reasonable opportunity to attend, even if the party fails to do so.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602 Licensing power of the state board -- Licensing final action -- Appeal rights.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(1): The state board holds the power to license educators.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(2)(a): The state board shall take final action with regard to an educator license.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(2)(b): An entity other than the state board may not take final action with regard to an educator license.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(3): (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(3)(a): (3)(b) In accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-602(3)(b): A license applicant or educator may file a petition for judicial review of the state board's final action if the license applicant or educator files a petition within 30 days after the day on which the license applicant or educator received notice of the final action.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-603(1)(b)(ii): a violation of standards of ethical conduct, performance, or professional competence.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(b)(vii)(B): is not a minor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(b)(vii)(C): is enrolled in an LEA where the educator is employed or is a participant in an extracurricular program in which the educator is involved; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(b)(viii): (5)(b)(v); (vi); (vii) admits to the state board or UPPAC that the applicant committed conduct that amounts to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(b)(viii)(A): a felony of a sexual nature; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(b)(viii)(B): (5)(b)(v); (vi); (vii) a sexual offense or sexually explicit conduct described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(c): The state board may not reinstate a revoked license.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-604(5)(d): Before the state board takes adverse action against an educator under this section, the state board shall ensure that the educator had an opportunity for a UPPAC hearing.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-605 Designation of hearing officer or panel -- Review of findings.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-605(1): UPPAC or a state or local school board charged with responsibility for conducting a hearing may conduct the hearing itself or appoint a hearing officer or panel to conduct the hearing and make recommendations concerning findings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-605(2): UPPAC or the local school board shall review the record of the hearing and the recommendations, and may obtain and review, in the presence of the parties or their representatives, additional relevant information, prior to issuing official findings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-605(3): UPPAC shall provide a panel of its members to serve as fact finders in a hearing at the request of the educator who is the subject of the hearing.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-606 Administering of oaths -- Issuance of subpoenas.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-606(1): UPPAC or a state or local school board charged with responsibility for conducting an investigation or a hearing under this chapter may administer oaths and issue subpoenas in connection with the investigation or hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-606(2): If a hearing is before a hearing officer or panel, the hearing officer or panel may administer oaths, and the appointing body may issue subpoenas upon the request of the hearing officer or panel.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-606(3): Subpoenas shall be enforced upon the petition of the issuing body by the district court in the jurisdiction where the subpoena was issued, in the same manner as subpoenas issued by the court.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607 Policies for conducting hearings -- Standard of proof.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(1): The state board and each local school board shall adopt policies for the conduct of hearings to ensure that requirements of due process are met.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(2): An accused party shall be provided not less than 15 days before a hearing with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(2)(a): notice of the hearing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(2)(b): the law, rule, or policy alleged to have been violated;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(2)(c): sufficient information about the allegations and the evidence to be presented in support of the allegations to permit the accused party to prepare a meaningful defense; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(2)(d): a copy of the policies under which the hearing will be conducted.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(3): If an accused party fails to request a hearing within 30 days after written notice is sent to the party's address as shown on the records of the local school board, for actions taken under the auspices of a local school board, or on the records of the state board, for actions taken under the auspices of the state board, then the accused party shall be considered to have waived the right to a hearing and the action may proceed without further delay.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(4): Hearing fact finders shall use the preponderance of evidence standard in deciding all questions unless a higher standard is required by law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-607(5): Unless otherwise provided in this public education code, the decisions of state and local school boards are final determinations under this section, appealable to the appropriate court for review.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701 Mandatory reporting of physical or sexual abuse of students.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701(1): 53E-6-102 For purposes of this section, "educator" means, in addition to a person included under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701(2): 80-2-602 In addition to any duty to report suspected cases of child abuse or neglect under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701(3): (2) A school administrator who has received a report under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701(4): (2); (3); 53E-6-604 Upon notice that an educator allegedly violated Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-701(5): A person who makes a report under this section in good faith shall be immune from civil or criminal liability that might otherwise arise by reason of that report.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702 Reimbursement of legal fees and costs to educators.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702(1): 52-6-201 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702(1)(a): 52-6-201 "Action" means any action, except those referred to in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702(1)(a)(i): the entity who licenses the educator; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702(1)(a)(ii): the LEA that employs the educator or employed the educator at the time of the alleged act or omission.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-6-702(1)(b): "Educator" means an individual who holds or is required to hold a license as defined by the state board and is employed by an LEA located within the state.
