Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409 Instructional Materials Access Center -- Board to make rules.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(1): The state board shall collaborate with the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind, school districts, and charter schools in establishing the Utah State Instructional Materials Access Center to provide students with print disabilities access to instructional materials in alternate formats in a timely manner.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The state board shall make rules, in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(a): establish the Utah State Instructional Materials Access Center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(b): define how the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind shall collaborate in the operation of the Utah State Instructional Materials Access Center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(c): specify procedures for the operation of the Utah State Instructional Materials Access Center, including procedures to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(c)(i): identify students who qualify for instructional materials in alternate formats; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(c)(ii): distribute and store instructional materials in alternate formats; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-409(2)(d): require textbook publishers, as a condition of contract, to provide electronic file sets in conformance with the National Instructional Materials Accessibility Standard.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-8-410 School districts to provide space for programs.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A school district with students who reside within the school district's boundaries and are served by the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind shall make a good faith effort to provide the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind with space required for programs offered by the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 9 - Student Privacy and Data Protection
*********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Student Privacy and Data Protection."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-201 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202 Application of state and federal law to the administration and operation of public schools -- Local school board and charter school governing board policies.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1): As used in this section "education entity" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1)(a): the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1)(b): a local school board or charter school governing board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1)(c): a school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1)(d): a public school; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(1)(e): the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(2): An education entity and an employee, student aide, volunteer, third party contractor, or other agent of an education entity shall protect the privacy of a student, the student's parents, and the student's family and support parental involvement in the education of their children through compliance with the protections provided for family and student privacy under this part and the Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act and related provisions under 20 U.S.C. Secs. 1232g and 1232h, in the administration and operation of all public school programs, regardless of the source of funding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-202(3): A local school board or charter school governing board shall enact policies governing the protection of family and student privacy as required by this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204 Access to education records -- Training requirement -- Certification.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(1): As used in this section, "education record" means the same as that term is defined in the Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1232g.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(2): (4); (2)(a) A local school board or charter school governing board shall require each public school to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(2)(a): (4) create and maintain a list that includes the name and position of each school employee who the public school authorizes, in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(2)(b): (2)(a) provide the list described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(3): (2); (3)(a); (3)(a) A local school board or charter school governing board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(3)(a): provide training on student privacy laws; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(3)(b): (2); (3)(a); (3)(a) require a school employee on the list described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(3)(b)(i): (3)(a) complete the training described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(3)(b)(ii): (3)(a) provide to the local school board or charter school governing board a certified statement, signed by the school employee, that certifies that the school employee completed the training described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4): (4)(b); (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(a): (4)(b); (2) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(a)(i): (2) that school employee's name is on the list described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(a)(ii): federal and state privacy laws authorize the education record to be shared with that school employee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(b): A local school board, charter school governing board, public school, or school employee may share an education record with a school employee if the board, school, or employee obtains written consent from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(b)(i): the parent of the student to whom the education record relates, if the student is younger than 18 years old; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-204(4)(b)(ii): the student to whom the education record relates, if the student is 18 years old or older.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205 Parental right to student information.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(1): 53E-9-204; 34A-5-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(1)(a): 53E-9-204 "Education record" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(1)(b): 34A-5-102 "Gender identity" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(1)(c): "Parent" means a parent or legal guardian with legal custody of the child in question.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(1)(d): "Sex" means the biological, physical condition of being male or female, determined by an individual's genetics and anatomy at birth.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(2): 53E-2-201; 53E-9-203(6) In accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(2)(a): 53E-9-203(6) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(2)(b): interferes with a parent's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(2)(b)(i): fundamental parental right and primary responsibility to direct the education of the parent's child; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(2)(b)(ii): freedom of access to information regarding the parent's child.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(3): Notwithstanding any other provision of law, a school or LEA may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(3)(a): prohibit a parent of a child from accessing the child's education record; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-205(3)(b): without written parental consent make changes to a student's education record regarding a student's gender identity that does not conform with the student's sex.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(1): "Adult student" means a student who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(1)(a): is at least 18 years old;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(1)(b): is an emancipated student; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(1)(c): qualifies under the McKinney-Vento Homeless Education Assistance Improvements Act of 2001, 42 U.S.C. Sec. 11431 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(2): "Aggregate data" means data that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(2)(a): are totaled and reported at the group, cohort, school, school district, region, or state level with at least 10 individuals in the level;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(2)(b): do not reveal personally identifiable student data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(2)(c): are collected in accordance with state board rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(a): "Biometric identifier" means a:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(a)(i): retina or iris scan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(a)(ii): fingerprint;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(a)(iii): human biological sample used for valid scientific testing or screening; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(a)(iv): scan of hand or face geometry.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b): "Biometric identifier" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(i): a writing sample;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(ii): a written signature;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(iii): a voiceprint;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(iv): a photograph;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(v): demographic data; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(3)(b)(vi): a physical description, such as height, weight, hair color, or eye color.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(4): "Biometric information" means information, regardless of how the information is collected, converted, stored, or shared:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(4)(a): based on an individual's biometric identifier; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(4)(b): used to identify the individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(5): "Data breach" means an unauthorized release of or unauthorized access to personally identifiable student data that is maintained by an education entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6): "Data governance plan" means an education entity's comprehensive plan for managing education data that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(a): incorporates reasonable data industry best practices to maintain and protect student data and other education-related data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(b): describes the role, responsibility, and authority of an education entity data governance staff member;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(c): provides for necessary technical assistance, training, support, and auditing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(d): describes the process for sharing student data between an education entity and another person;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(e): describes the education entity's data expungement process, including how to respond to requests for expungement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(f): describes the data breach response process; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(6)(g): is published annually and available on the education entity's website.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7): "Education entity" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(a): the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(b): a local school board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(c): a charter school governing board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(d): a school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(e): a charter school; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(7)(f): the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(8): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; 53E-9-306 "Expunge" means to seal or permanently delete data, as described in state board rule made in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(9): "General audience application" means an Internet website, online service, online application, mobile application, or software program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(9)(a): is not specifically intended for use by an audience member that attends kindergarten or a grade from 1 to 12, although an audience member may attend kindergarten or a grade from 1 to 12; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(9)(b): is not subject to a contract between an education entity and a third-party contractor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(10): "Local education agency" or "LEA" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(10)(a): a school district;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(10)(b): a charter school; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(10)(c): the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11): "Metadata dictionary" means a record that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(a): defines and discloses all personally identifiable student data collected and shared by the education entity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(b): comprehensively lists all recipients with whom the education entity has shared personally identifiable student data, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(b)(i): the purpose for sharing the data with the recipient;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(b)(ii): the justification for sharing the data, including whether sharing the data was required by federal law, state law, or a local directive; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(b)(iii): how sharing the data is permitted under federal or state law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(11)(c): without disclosing personally identifiable student data, is displayed on the education entity's website.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12): 53G-9-404; 53G-9-404; 26B-7-115; 53E-9-306 "Necessary student data" means data required by state statute or federal law to conduct the regular activities of an education entity, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(a): name;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(b): date of birth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(c): sex;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(d): parent contact information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(e): custodial parent information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(f): contact information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(g): a student identification number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(h): local, state, and national assessment results or an exception from taking a local, state, or national assessment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(i): courses taken and completed, credits earned, and other transcript information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(j): course grades and grade point average;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(k): grade level and expected graduation date or graduation cohort;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(l): degree, diploma, credential attainment, and other school exit information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(m): attendance and mobility;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(n): drop-out data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(o): immunization record or an exception from an immunization record;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(p): race;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(q): ethnicity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(r): tribal affiliation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(s): remediation efforts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(t): 53G-9-404; 53G-9-404 an exception from a vision screening required under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(u): 26B-7-115 information related to the Utah Registry of Autism and Developmental Disabilities, described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(v): student injury information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(w): 53E-9-306 a disciplinary record created and maintained as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(x): juvenile delinquency records;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(y): English language learner status; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(12)(z): child find and special education evaluation data related to initiation of an IEP.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13): 53E-9-305
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(a): 53E-9-305 "Optional student data" means student data that is not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(a)(i): necessary student data; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(a)(ii): 53E-9-305 student data that an education entity may not collect under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b): "Optional student data" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b)(i): information that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b)(i)(A): related to an IEP or needed to provide special needs services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b)(i)(B): not necessary student data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b)(ii): biometric information; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(13)(b)(iii): information that is not necessary student data and that is required for a student to participate in a federal or other program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(14): "Parent" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(14)(a): a student's parent;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(14)(b): a student's legal guardian; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(14)(c): an individual who has written authorization from a student's parent or legal guardian to act as a parent or legal guardian on behalf of the student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(a): "Personally identifiable student data" means student data that identifies or is used by the holder to identify a student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b): "Personally identifiable student data" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(i): a student's first and last name;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(ii): the first and last name of a student's family member;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(iii): a student's or a student's family's home or physical address;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(iv): a student's email address or other online contact information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(v): a student's telephone number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(vi): a student's social security number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(vii): a student's biometric identifier;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(viii): a student's health or disability data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(ix): a student's education entity student identification number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(x): a student's social media user name and password or alias;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xi): if associated with personally identifiable student data, the student's persistent identifier, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xi)(A): a customer number held in a cookie; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xi)(B): a processor serial number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xii): a combination of a student's last name or photograph with other information that together permits a person to contact the student online;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xiii): information about a student or a student's family that a person collects online and combines with other personally identifiable student data to identify the student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(15)(b)(xiv): information that, alone or in combination, is linked or linkable to a specific student that would allow a reasonable person in the school community, who does not have personal knowledge of the relevant circumstances, to identify the student with reasonable certainty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(16): "School official" means an employee or agent of an education entity, if the education entity has authorized the employee or agent to request or receive student data on behalf of the education entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(17): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(17)(a): "Student data" means information about a student at the individual student level.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(17)(b): "Student data" does not include aggregate or de-identified data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(18): 53E-9-303; 53E-9-308 "Student data manager" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(18)(a): the state student data officer; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(18)(b): 53E-9-303; 53E-9-308 an individual designated as a student data manager by an education entity under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(19): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(19)(a): "Targeted advertising" means presenting advertisements to a student where the advertisement is selected based on information obtained or inferred over time from that student's online behavior, usage of applications, or student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(19)(b): "Targeted advertising" does not include advertising to a student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(19)(b)(i): at an online location based upon that student's current visit to that location; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(19)(b)(ii): in response to that student's request for information or feedback, without retention of that student's online activities or requests over time for the purpose of targeting subsequent ads.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(20): "Third-party contractor" means a person who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(20)(a): is not an education entity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(20)(b): pursuant to a contract with an education entity, collects or receives student data in order to provide a product or service, as described in the contract, if the product or service is not related to school photography, yearbooks, graduation announcements, or a similar product or service.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(21): "Written consent" means written authorization to collect or share a student's student data, from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(21)(a): the student's parent, if the student is not an adult student; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-301(21)(b): the student, if the student is an adult student.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302 State student data protection governance.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(1)(a): An education entity or a third-party contractor who collects, uses, stores, shares, or deletes student data shall protect student data as described in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(1)(b): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(2): The state board shall oversee the preparation and maintenance of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(2)(a): a statewide data governance plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(2)(b): a state-level metadata dictionary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3): (3) As described in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a): a student data policy advisory group:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(i): that is composed of members from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(i)(A): the Legislature;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(i)(B): the state board and state board employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(i)(C): one or more LEAs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(ii): to discuss and make recommendations to the state board regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(ii)(A): enacted or proposed legislation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(ii)(B): state and local student data protection policies across the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(iii): that reviews and monitors the state student data governance plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(a)(iv): that performs other tasks related to student data protection as designated by the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(b): a student data governance advisory group:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(b)(i): that is composed of the state student data officer and other state board employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(b)(ii): that performs duties related to state and local student data protection, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(b)(ii)(A): overseeing data collection and usage by state board program offices; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(b)(ii)(B): preparing and maintaining the state board's student data governance plan under the direction of the student data policy advisory group.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(c): a student data users advisory group:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(c)(i): that is composed of members who use student data at the local level; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(3)(c)(ii): that provides feedback and suggestions on the practicality of actions proposed by the student data policy advisory group and the student data governance advisory group.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(a): The state board shall designate a state student data officer.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b): The state student data officer shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(i): act as the primary point of contact for state student data protection administration in assisting the state board to administer this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(ii): ensure compliance with student privacy laws throughout the public education system, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(ii)(A): providing training and support to applicable state board and LEA employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(ii)(B): producing resource materials, model plans, and model forms for local student data protection governance, including a model student data collection notice;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(iii): investigate complaints of alleged violations of this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(iv): report violations of this part to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(iv)(A): the state board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(iv)(B): an applicable education entity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(iv)(C): the student data policy advisory group; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(4)(b)(v): act as a state level student data manager.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(5): The state board shall designate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(5)(a): at least one support manager to assist the state student data officer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(5)(b): a student data protection auditor to assist the state student data officer.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-302(6): The state board shall establish a research review process for a request for data for the purpose of research or evaluation.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303 Local student data protection governance.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(1): An LEA shall adopt policies to protect student data in accordance with this part and state board rule, taking into account the specific needs and priorities of the LEA.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(2): 53E-9-308; 63G-2-103
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(2)(a): 53E-9-308 An LEA shall designate an individual to act as a student data manager to fulfill the responsibilities of a student data manager described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(2)(b): 63G-2-103 If possible, an LEA shall designate the LEA's records officer as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(3): An LEA shall create and maintain an LEA:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(3)(a): data governance plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(3)(b): metadata dictionary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-303(4): An LEA shall establish an external research review process for a request for data for the purpose of external research or evaluation.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304 Student data ownership and access -- Notification in case of significant data breach.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1): 53E-9-303
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1)(a): A student owns the student's personally identifiable student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1)(b): 53E-9-303 An education entity shall allow the following individuals to access a student's student data that is maintained by the education entity:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1)(b)(i): the student's parent;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1)(b)(ii): the student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(1)(b)(iii): 53E-9-303 in accordance with the education entity's internal policy described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(2): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(2)(a): If a significant data breach occurs at an education entity, the education entity shall notify:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(2)(a)(i): the student, if the student is an adult student; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(2)(a)(ii): the student's parent, if the student is not an adult student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-304(2)(b): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (2)(a) In accordance with

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
"The collection, use, and sharing of student data has both benefits and risks.  Parents and students should learn about these benefits and risks and make choices regarding student data accordingly.";Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-305(1): 80-6-103 An education entity may not collect a student's:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-305(1)(b): 80-6-103 except as required in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-305(2)(a): is a prominent, stand-alone document;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-305(2)(b): is annually updated and published on the education entity's website;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-305(2)(c): states the student data that the education entity collects;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309 Third-party contractors.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(1): A third-party contractor shall use personally identifiable student data received under a contract with an education entity strictly for the purpose of providing the contracted product or service within the negotiated contract terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2): (4) When contracting with a third-party contractor, an education entity, or a government agency contracting on behalf of an education entity, shall require the following provisions in the contract:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2)(a): requirements and restrictions related to the collection, use, storage, or sharing of student data by the third-party contractor that are necessary for the education entity to ensure compliance with the provisions of this part and state board rule;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2)(b): a description of a person, or type of person, including an affiliate of the third-party contractor, with whom the third-party contractor may share student data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2)(c): provisions that, at the request of the education entity, govern the deletion of the student data received by the third-party contractor;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2)(d): (4) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(2)(e): an agreement by the third-party contractor that, at the request of the education entity that is a party to the contract, the education entity or the education entity's designee may audit the third-party contractor to verify compliance with the contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(3): As authorized by law or court order, a third-party contractor shall share student data as requested by law enforcement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4): A third-party contractor may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(a): use student data for adaptive learning or customized student learning purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(b): market an educational application or product to a parent of a student if the third-party contractor did not use student data, shared by or collected on behalf of an education entity, to market the educational application or product;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(c): use a recommendation engine to recommend to a student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(c)(i): content that relates to learning or employment, within the third-party contractor's application, if the recommendation is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(c)(ii): services that relate to learning or employment, within the third-party contractor's application, if the recommendation is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(d): respond to a student request for information or feedback, if the content of the response is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(e): use student data to allow or improve operability and functionality of the third-party contractor's application; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(f): identify for a student nonprofit institutions of higher education or scholarship providers that are seeking students who meet specific criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(f)(i): regardless of whether the identified nonprofit institutions of higher education or scholarship providers provide payment or other consideration to the third-party contractor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(f)(ii): only if the third-party contractor obtains authorization in writing from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(f)(ii)(A): a student's parent through the student's school or LEA; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(4)(f)(ii)(B): for an adult student, the student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(5): At the completion of a contract with an education entity, if the contract has not been renewed, a third-party contractor shall return or delete upon the education entity's request all personally identifiable student data under the control of the education entity unless a student or the student's parent consents to the maintenance of the personally identifiable student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6): (6)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6)(a): (6)(b) A third-party contractor may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6)(a)(i): (6)(b) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6)(a)(ii): collect, use, or share student data, if the collection, use, or sharing of the student data is inconsistent with the third-party contractor's contract with the education entity; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6)(a)(iii): use student data for targeted advertising.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(6)(b): A person may obtain student data through the purchase of, merger with, or otherwise acquiring a third-party contractor if the third-party contractor remains in compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(7): The provisions of this section do not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(7)(a): apply to the use of a general audience application, including the access of a general audience application with login credentials created by a third-party contractor's application;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(7)(b): apply if the student data is shared in accordance with the education entity's directory information policy, as described in 34 C.F.R. 99.37;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(7)(c): apply to the providing of Internet service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(7)(d): impose a duty on a provider of an interactive computer service, as defined in 47 U.S.C. Sec. 230, to review or enforce compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(8): A provision of this section that relates to a student's student data does not apply to a third-party contractor if the education entity or third-party contractor obtains authorization from the following individual, in writing, to waive that provision:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(8)(a): the student's parent, if the student is not an adult student; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-309(8)(b): the student, if the student is an adult student.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310 Penalties.
------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1): (1)(b); (1)(a)(ii); Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act; (1)(a)(ii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a): (1)(b) A third-party contractor that knowingly or recklessly permits unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data under this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a)(i): (1)(b) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a)(ii): may be required by the state board to pay a civil penalty of up to $25,000; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a)(iii): may be required to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a)(iii)(A): the education entity's cost of notifying parents and students of the unauthorized sharing or use of student data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(a)(iii)(B): expenses incurred by the education entity as a result of the unauthorized sharing or use of student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(b): An education entity may enter into a contract with a third-party contractor that knowingly or recklessly permitted unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(b)(i): the state board or education entity determines that the third-party contractor has corrected the errors that caused the unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(b)(ii): the third-party contractor demonstrates:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(b)(ii)(A): if the third-party contractor is under contract with an education entity, current compliance with this part; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(b)(ii)(B): an ability to comply with the requirements of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(c): (1)(a)(ii); Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act The state board may assess the civil penalty described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(d): (1)(a)(ii) The state board may bring an action in the district court of the county in which the office of the state board is located, if necessary, to enforce payment of the civil penalty described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(1)(e): An individual who knowingly or intentionally permits unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data may be found guilty of a class A misdemeanor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(2): 53E-9-309; 53E-9-309
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(2)(a): 53E-9-309 A parent or adult student may bring an action in a court of competent jurisdiction for damages caused by a knowing or reckless violation of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(2)(b): 53E-9-309 If the court finds that a third-party contractor has violated Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(2)(b)(i): damages; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-9-310(2)(b)(ii): costs.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53E - Chapter 10 - Other Programs
*************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Other Programs."

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202 State board to supervise.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(1): The general control and supervision, but not the direct management, of adult education is vested in the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(2): The state board has the following powers:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(2)(a): makes and enforces rules to organize, conduct, and supervise adult education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(2)(b): appoints state staff for the adult education program, establishes their duties, and fixes their compensation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(2)(c): determines the qualifications of, and issues teaching certificates to, persons employed to give adult education instruction; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(2)(d): determines the basis of apportionment and distributes funds made available for adult education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(3): 53G-7-504; 53G-7-505
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(3)(a): The state board shall make rules providing for the establishment of fees which shall be imposed by local school boards for participation in adult education programs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(3)(b): A fee structure for adult education shall take into account the ability of a Utah resident who participates in adult education to pay the fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-202(3)(c): 53G-7-504; 53G-7-505 Sections


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-203 Director of adult education.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-203(1): Upon recommendation of the state superintendent, the state board may appoint a full-time director for adult education to work under the supervision of the state board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-203(2): 53E-10-202; 53E-10-206 The director may coordinate the adult education program authorized under Sections


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-204 Local school boards' authority to direct adult education programs.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A local school board may do the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-204(1): establish and maintain classes for adult education, with classes being held at times and places convenient and accessible to the members of the class;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-204(2): raise and appropriate funds for an adult education program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-204(3): 53E-10-202 subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-204(4): hire persons to instruct adult education classes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-205 Eligibility.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-205(1): Adult education classes are open to an individual 16 years of age or over and to an individual who has completed high school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-205(2): Eligible nonresidents of the state shall be charged tuition at least equal to that charged nonresident students for similar classes at a local or nearby state college or university, unless waived in whole or in part by the local school board in an open meeting.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-205(3): The district superintendent may, upon the recommendation of an authorized representative of the Division of Child and Family Services, exempt an adult domiciled in Utah from the payment of adult education fees.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-206 Salaries -- Costs.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-206(1): Salaries and other necessary expenses of the state adult education staff shall be paid from funds appropriated for adult education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-206(2): The state board shall determine the terms and conditions of payment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-206(3): A local school board shall pay all costs incident to the local administration and operation of its adult education program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-206(4): The local school board shall submit reports required by the state board for the administration of adult education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-301(5)(c): is in grade 9, 10, 11, or 12.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-301(10): "Value of the weighted pupil unit" means the amount established each year in the enacted public education budget that is multiplied by the number of weighted pupil units to yield the funding level for the basic state-supported school program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-302 Concurrent enrollment program.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-302(1): 53E-10-307; (3) The state board and the Utah Board of Higher Education shall establish and maintain a concurrent enrollment program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-302(1)(a): provides an eligible student the opportunity to enroll in a course that allows the eligible student to earn credit concurrently:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-302(1)(a)(i): toward high school graduation; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-701(3)(b): school; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-701(3)(c): charter school.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-701(6)(a): advises the director;

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-701(6)(c): 53E-10-707 is created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702 ULEAD established -- Duties -- Funding.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
There is created the Utah Leading through Effective, Actionable, and Dynamic Education, a collaborative effort in research and innovation between the director, participating institutions, and education leaders to:Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(1): gather and explain current education research in an electronic research clearinghouse for use by practitioners;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(2): initiate and disseminate research reports on innovative and successful practices by Utah LEAs, and guided by the steering committee, practitioners, and policymakers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(3): promote statewide innovation and collaboration by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(3)(a): identifying experts in areas of practice;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(3)(b): conducting conferences, webinars, and online forums for practitioners; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(3)(c): facilitating direct collaboration between schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(4)(a): report to the Education Interim Committee and policymakers on innovative and successful K-12 practices in Utah and other states, prioritizing practices in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-702(4)(b): in the report, propose policy changes to remove barriers to implementation of successful practices.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703 ULEAD director -- Qualification and employment -- Duties -- Reporting -- Annual conference.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1): The ULEAD director shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(a)(i): hold a doctorate degree in education or an equivalent degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(a)(ii): have demonstrated experience in research and dissemination of best practices in education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(b)(i): be a full-time employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(b)(ii): report to the state superintendent; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(1)(b)(iii): provide a report to the selection committee, at least twice per year, on the status of the ULEAD program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(2): The state superintendent shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(2)(a): evaluate the director's performance annually;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(2)(b): report on the director's performance to the selection committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(2)(c): provide space for the director and the director's staff.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(3): The director may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(3)(a): hire staff, using only money specifically appropriated to ULEAD; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(3)(b): with approval from the superintendent, utilize state board staff.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4): The director shall perform the following duties and functions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(a): gather current research on innovative and effective practices in K-12 education for use by policymakers and practitioners;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(b): facilitate collaboration between LEAs, higher education researchers, and practitioners by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(b)(i): sharing innovative and effective practices in Utah shown to improve student learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(b)(ii): identifying experts in Utah in specific areas of practice; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(b)(iii): maintaining a research clearinghouse and directory of researchers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(4)(c): analyze barriers to replication or adaption of innovative and successful practices studied by ULEAD or contributed to the ULEAD research clearinghouse.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5): 53E-10-707(5); 53E-10-707(6) The director shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(a): 53E-10-707(5); 53E-10-707(6) prioritize reports and other research based on recommendations of the steering committee in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(b): identify Utah LEAs, or schools outside the public school system, that are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(b)(i): innovative in specific areas of practice; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(b)(ii): more effective or efficient than comparable LEAs in improving student learning, especially for students performing below proficiency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(c): establish criteria for innovative practice reports to be performed by participating institutions and included in the research clearinghouse, including report templates;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(d): arrange with participating institutions to generate innovative practice reports on effective and innovative K-12 education practices; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(e): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(e)(i): disseminate each innovative practice report to the state board for dissemination to LEAs and school leaders; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(5)(e)(ii): publish innovative practice reports on the ULEAD website.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6): In an innovative practice report, a participating institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(a): include or reference a review of research regarding the practice in which the subject LEA has demonstrated success;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(b): identify through academically acceptable, evidence-based research methods the causes of the LEA's successful practice;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(c): identify opportunities for LEAs to adopt or customize innovative or best practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(d): address limitations to successful replication or adaptation of the successful practice by other LEAs, which may include barriers arising from federal or state law, state or LEA policy, socioeconomic conditions, or funding limitations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(e): include practical templates for successful replication and adaptation of successful practices, following criteria established by the director;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(f): identify experts in the successful practice that is the subject of the innovative practice report, including teachers or administrators at the subject LEA; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(g): include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(g)(i): an executive summary describing the innovative practice report; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-703(6)(g)(ii): a video component or other elements designed to ensure that an innovative practice report is readily understandable by practitioners.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704 Director Selection Committee -- Membership -- Powers and duties -- Compensation.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(1): There is created the Director Selection Committee to appoint the director.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2): The selection committee shall consist of the following five members each appointed for two-year terms:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2)(a): one member of the office of the governor, who is the chair of the selection committee and appointed by the governor;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2)(b): one member of the House of Representatives, appointed by the speaker of the House of Representatives;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2)(c): one member of the Senate, appointed by the president of the Senate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2)(d): one member of the state board, appointed by the chair of the state board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(2)(e): one member appointed by the state superintendent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(3): (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(3)(a): A member of the selection committee may be appointed for more than one term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(3)(b): (2) If a midterm vacancy occurs on the selection committee, the appointing individual, as described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(4): A majority of the members shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of selection committee business.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(5)(a): The selection committee shall select and appoint a director for a four-year term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(5)(b): The director may be appointed for more than one term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6): (6)(b); (c); (6)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(a): (6)(b); (c) In addition to the meetings required under Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(b): In a year in which the director is appointed, the selection committee shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(b)(i): solicit applications for the director position to be submitted no later than June 1;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(b)(ii): hold at least two meetings to discuss candidates for the open director position; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(b)(iii): select and appoint by majority vote a candidate to fill the director position to begin employment no later than August 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(c): (6)(b) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(c)(i): no later than 25 business days after the day on which the position is vacated, solicit applications for the director position;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(c)(ii): hold at least two meetings to discuss candidates for the vacant position; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(6)(c)(iii): no later than 60 business days after the day on which the position is vacated, select a candidate to fill the director position for the remainder of the term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(7)(a): The selection committee:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(7)(a)(i): may remove a director before the completion of the director's term only by a majority vote of the selection committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(7)(a)(ii): is the only person empowered to remove the director.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(7)(b): The chair shall hold a meeting to consider removing the director upon request of two or more selection committee members.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(9): The selection committee shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(9)(a): establish criteria for evaluation of the ULEAD program, including the degree of participation by participating institutions and practitioners;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(9)(b): evaluate the effectiveness of ULEAD every four years for purposes of continuing the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-704(9)(c): meet with the superintendent at least annually to discuss the progress of ULEAD projects and processes as described in this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705 Participating institutions.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; 53G-7-202 The director may arrange or collaborate with a participating institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(a): to conduct an innovative practice report or provide other research services, including research regarding barriers to adoption of practices studied by ULEAD;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(b): to assist an LEA to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(b)(i): facilitate communities of practice for replication or adaptation of best practices identified by ULEAD; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(b)(ii): advise teachers and school leaders on conducting their own research to improve education practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(c): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; 53G-7-202 to assist an LEA with an application to the state board for waiver from a state board rule, made in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(1)(d): for any other purpose that is consistent with and advances the director's duties and functions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(2): An agreement entered into by a participating institution with the state board or an LEA to perform ULEAD work shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(2)(a): include provisions allowing and governing external research data sharing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(2)(b): comply with state and federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-705(3): The director shall support federal and private research funding requests by a participating institution for research that is in support of the director's duties and functions.


Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706 Electronic resources -- Research clearinghouse.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(1): The state board shall publish a ULEAD website containing information provided by the director as described in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2): (1); 53B-33-201 The director shall within two years of appointment:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(a): (1) develop and maintain a research clearinghouse publicly available through the website described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b): 53B-33-201 include in the research clearinghouse:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(i): research on K-12 education, including peer-reviewed research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(ii): information on K-12 education innovation and best practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(iii): an index and explanation of academic, state, federal, or other K-12 education research repositories;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(iv): K-12 education research and policy briefs generated by Utah public and private institutions of higher education, including participating institutions, categorized and searchable by topic;
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(v): 53B-33-201 access points to and explanation of currently available K-12 education data, including data managed by the Utah Data Research Center created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(vi): other K-12 education information as determined by the director, including information regarding efforts by institutions or other individuals to promote innovative and effective education practices in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(2)(b)(vii): each innovative practice report prepared by ULEAD, categorized and searchable by topic, location of the studied LEA, and socioeconomic and demographic profile.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(3): 53E-10-703(5)(b) The director shall publish:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(3)(a): 53E-10-703(5)(b) as identified in ULEAD research and reports, an electronic directory of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(3)(a)(i): K-12 education experts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(3)(a)(ii): 53E-10-703(5)(b) LEAs described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(3)(b): a monthly report to LEAs, via electronic channels provided by the state board, highlighting ULEAD activities and soliciting proposals from education practitioners for ULEAD research and reports.
Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-706(4): The director may provide electronic seminars or forums for professional learning regarding subjects of ULEAD research and reports to K-12 practitioners.

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-707(2): Chapter 6, Education Professional Licensure The steering committee shall consist of the following members each appointed for a term of two years:

Utah Code Annotated § 53E-10-707(2)(k): one member representing citizens or business, nominated by the members of the public and appointed by the director.
